  spring (ModuleScript)
    Path: game.ReplicatedStorage.include.node_modules.@rbxts.ripple.src.solvers.spring

    local config = require(script.Parent.Parent.config)
    local intermediate = require(script.Parent.Parent.utils.intermediate)
    local function configure(p1) --[[ configure | Line: 8 | Upvalues: config (copy) ]]

    	local v2 = p1.tension or config.spring.default.tension
    	local v3 = p1.friction or config.spring.default.friction

    		local v4 = p1.frequency or 0.5
    		v3 = 12.566370614359172 * (p1.damping or 1) * v1 / v4
    		v2 = (6.283185307179586 / v4) ^ 2 * v1
    	return {
    		mass = v1,
    		tension = v2,
    		friction = v3,

    		velocity = p1.velocity,

    	}
    return function(p1, p2) --[[ spring | Line: 32 | Upvalues: configure (copy), intermediate (copy) ]]

    			local sum = p2.velocity or 0
    			for i = 1, math.min(math.ceil(p3 * 1000 / 1), 100) do
    				sum = sum + (-v3.tension * 1e-6 * (value - v1) + -v3.friction * 0.001 * sum) / v3.mass * 1

    			if math.abs(sum) < v3.restingVelocity and math.abs(value - v1) < v3.restingPosition then
